Benchmarks for decomposition¶

RandomizedPCA-arcene¶

Benchmark setup

from sklearn.decomposition import RandomizedPCA
from deps import load_data

kwargs = {'random_state': 0, 'n_components': 9}
X, y, X_t, y_t = load_data('arcene')
obj = RandomizedPCA(**kwargs)

Benchmark statement

obj.fit(X)

   216                                                       and n_features is the number of features.
   217
   218                                                   Returns
   219                                                   -------
   220                                                   X_new : array-like, shape (n_samples, n_components)
   221
   222                                                   """
   223                                                   U, S, V = self._fit(X)
   224                                                   U = U[:, :self.n_components_]
   225
   226                                                   if self.whiten:
   227                                                       # X_new = X * V / S * sqrt(n_samples) = U * sqrt(n_samples)
   228                                                       U *= sqrt(X.shape[0])
   229                                                   else:
   230                                                       # X_new = X * V = U * S * V^T * V = U * S
   231                                                       U *= S[:self.n_components_]
   232
   233                                                   return U

   209                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None):
   210                                                   """Fit the model with X and apply the dimensionality reduction on X.
   211
   212                                                   Parameters
   213                                                   ----------
   214                                                   X : array-like, shape (n_samples, n_features)
   215                                                       Training data, where n_samples is the number of samples
   216                                                       and n_features is the number of features.
   217
   218                                                   Returns
   219                                                   -------
   220                                                   X_new : array-like, shape (n_samples, n_components)
   221
   222                                                   """
   223         1      2282477 2282477.0    100.0          U, S, V = self._fit(X)
   224         1            7      7.0      0.0          U = U[:, :self.n_components_]
   225
   226         1            2      2.0      0.0          if self.whiten:
   227                                                       # X_new = X * V / S * sqrt(n_samples) = U * sqrt(n_samples)
   228                                                       U *= sqrt(X.shape[0])
   229                                                   else:
   230                                                       # X_new = X * V = U * S * V^T * V = U * S
   231         1          105    105.0      0.0              U *= S[:self.n_components_]
   232
   233         1            2      2.0      0.0          return U

   336                                               def fit(self, X, y=None, homoscedastic=True):
   337                                                   """Additionally to PCA.fit, learns a covariance model
   338
   339                                                   Parameters
   340                                                   ----------
   341                                                   X : array of shape(n_samples, n_features)
   342                                                       The data to fit
   343
   344                                                   homoscedastic : bool, optional,
   345                                                       If True, average variance across remaining dimensions
   346                                                   """
   347         1      2291540 2291540.0     97.9          PCA.fit(self, X)
   348         1            5      5.0      0.0          n_samples, n_features = X.shape
   349         1            3      3.0      0.0          self._dim = n_features
   350         1         4116   4116.0      0.2          Xr = X - self.mean_
   351         1        34058  34058.0      1.5          Xr -= np.dot(np.dot(Xr, self.components_.T), self.components_)
   352
   353         1            4      4.0      0.0          n_components = self.n_components
   354         1            4      4.0      0.0          if n_components is None:
   355                                                       n_components = n_features
   356
   357                                                   # Make the low rank part of the estimated covariance
   358         1           15     15.0      0.0          self.covariance_ = np.dot(self.components_[:n_components].T *
   359         1          121    121.0      0.0                                    self.explained_variance_[:n_components],
   360         1         4105   4105.0      0.2                                    self.components_[:n_components])
   361
   362         1            4      4.0      0.0          if n_features == n_components:
   363                                                       delta = 0.
   364         1            2      2.0      0.0          elif homoscedastic:
   365         1         5701   5701.0      0.2              delta = (Xr ** 2).sum() / (n_samples * n_features)
   366                                                   else:
   367                                                       delta = (Xr ** 2).mean(axis=0) / (n_features - n_components)
   368
   369                                                   # Add delta to the diagonal without extra allocation
   370         1           87     87.0      0.0          self.covariance_.flat[::n_features + 1] += delta

   567                                               def transform(self, X):
   568                                                   """Transform the data X according to the fitted NMF model
   569
   570                                                   Parameters
   571                                                   ----------
   572
   573                                                   X: {array-like, sparse matrix}, shape = [n_samples, n_features]
   574                                                       Data matrix to be transformed by the model
   575
   576                                                   Returns
   577                                                   -------
   578                                                   data: array, [n_samples, n_components]
   579                                                       Transformed data
   580                                                   """
   581                                                   X, = check_arrays(X, sparse_format='csc')
   582                                                   Wt = np.zeros((self.n_components_, X.shape[0]))
   583                                                   if sp.issparse(X):
   584                                                       Wt, _, _ = _nls_subproblem(X.T, self.components_.T, Wt,
   585                                                                                  tol=self.tol,
   586                                                                                  max_iter=self.nls_max_iter)
   587                                                   else:
   588                                                       for j in range(0, X.shape[0]):
   589                                                           Wt[:, j], _ = nnls(self.components_.T, X[j, :])
   590                                                   return Wt.T

   387                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **fit_params):
   388                                                   """Fit to data, then transform it.
   389
   390                                                   Fits transformer to X and y with optional parameters fit_params
   391                                                   and returns a transformed version of X.
   392
   393                                                   Parameters
   394                                                   ----------
   395                                                   X : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features]
   396                                                       Training set.
   397
   398                                                   y : numpy array of shape [n_samples]
   399                                                       Target values.
   400
   401                                                   Returns
   402                                                   -------
   403                                                   X_new : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features_new]
   404                                                       Transformed array.
   405
   406                                                   """
   407                                                   # non-optimized default implementation; override when a better
   408                                                   # method is possible for a given clustering algorithm
   409                                                   if y is None:
   410                                                       # fit method of arity 1 (unsupervised transformation)
   411                                                       return self.fit(X, **fit_params).transform(X)
   412                                                   else:
   413                                                       # fit method of arity 2 (supervised transformation)
   414                                                       return self.fit(X, y, **fit_params).transform(X)

Line #      Hits         Time  Per Hit   % Time  Line Contents
==============================================================
   679                                               def transform(self, X, y=None):
   680                                                   """Encode the data as a sparse combination of the dictionary atoms.
   681
   682                                                   Coding method is determined by the object parameter
   683                                                   `transform_algorithm`.
   684
   685                                                   Parameters
   686                                                   ----------
   687                                                   X : array of shape (n_samples, n_features)
   688                                                       Test data to be transformed, must have the same number of
   689                                                       features as the data used to train the model.
   690
   691                                                   Returns
   692                                                   -------
   693                                                   X_new : array, shape (n_samples, n_components)
   694                                                       Transformed data
   695
   696                                                   """
   697                                                   # XXX : kwargs is not documented
   698                                                   X = array2d(X)
   699                                                   n_samples, n_features = X.shape
   700
   701                                                   code = sparse_encode(
   702                                                       X, self.components_, algorithm=self.transform_algorithm,
   703                                                       n_nonzero_coefs=self.transform_n_nonzero_coefs,
   704                                                       alpha=self.transform_alpha, n_jobs=self.n_jobs)
   705
   706                                                   if self.split_sign:
   707                                                       # feature vector is split into a positive and negative side
   708                                                       n_samples, n_features = code.shape
   709                                                       split_code = np.empty((n_samples, 2 * n_features))
   710                                                       split_code[:, :n_features] = np.maximum(code, 0)
   711                                                       split_code[:, n_features:] = -np.minimum(code, 0)
   712                                                       code = split_code
   713
   714                                                   return code

   387                                               def fit_transform(self, X, y=None, **fit_params):
   388                                                   """Fit to data, then transform it.
   389
   390                                                   Fits transformer to X and y with optional parameters fit_params
   391                                                   and returns a transformed version of X.
   392
   393                                                   Parameters
   394                                                   ----------
   395                                                   X : numpy array of shape [n_samples, n_features]
   396                                                       Training set.

   399                                                       Target values.
   400
   401                                                   Returns
   402                                                   -------

   404                                                       Transformed array.
   405
   406                                                   """
   407                                                   # non-optimized default implementation; override when a better
   408                                                   # method is possible for a given clustering algorithm
   409                                                   if y is None:
   410                                                       # fit method of arity 1 (unsupervised transformation)
   411                                                       return self.fit(X, **fit_params).transform(X)

   413                                                       # fit method of arity 2 (supervised transformation)
   414                                                       return self.fit(X, y, **fit_params).transform(X)
